      <Execute displayName="RIC">
        <expr><![CDATA[if (Strcmp(SubString(Name, 1, 1), "/"))
	return StrReplace(Name, "/", "");
else
		return StoreString("RIC", Name);]]></expr>
      </Execute>
      <Execute displayName="DOMEN_CURR_CDE">
        <expr><![CDATA[return StoreString("DOMEN_CURR_CDE", Select("", "", "select distinct denom_curr_cde from ft_t_issu where instr_id = (select instr_id from ft_t_isid where id_ctxt_typ='RIC' and iss_id =:1 and (end_tms is null or end_tms > sysdate))", Name, "", "", "", ""));]]></expr>
      </Execute>
      <Execute displayName="CURR_CODE">
        <expr><![CDATA[return StoreString("CURR_CDE", If(OneHasValue(GetStringByKey("DOMEN_CURR_CDE")), GetStringByKey("DOMEN_CURR_CDE"), If(FieldPresent(CURRENCY) && !StrContainsOneOf(SubString(CURRENCY, 1, 3), "(", ")"), SubString(CURRENCY, 1, 3), "")));]]></expr>
      </Execute>
      <Execute displayName="LAST_CHG_USR_ID">

      <Execute displayName="TMS">
        <expr><![CDATA[return StoreString("TMS", If(OneHasValue(QUOTIM), If(StrLen(StrTrimLeft(StrTrimRight(QUOTIM))) < 8, Strcat(SubString(StrTrimLeft(StrTrimRight(QUOTIM)),1,5),":00"), QUOTIM), ""));]]></expr>
      </Execute>
      <Execute displayName="PRICE_DATE">
        <expr><![CDATA[return StoreString("PRICE_DATE", If(OneHasValue(QUOTE_DATE), Strcat(QUOTE_DATE, Strcat(" ", "00:00:00")), ""));]]></expr>
      </Execute>
